20/11/2024, 11:59â€¯am - Karn: Device Health Report
Idea: When donors upload device details, include an option for them to upload a basic health report of the device (battery life, screen condition, etc.).
How it Helps: It allows the system to prioritize devices needing less repair and helps match better devices with student needs.
Implementation: Add a form field during donation and display this report on the admin panel.

Reward System for Donors
Idea: Introduce a reward system where donors earn points or certificates for donating devices.
How it Helps: Encourages more people to donate by recognizing their contributions.
Implementation: Add a simple badge/certificate generator using Flutter and Firebase to email or display certificates after successful donations.


Blockchain for Donation Transparency
Idea: Use blockchain to track each device from donation to distribution. Users can see the journey of their donated devices, ensuring transparency.
How it Helps: Builds trust among donors and makes the process more accountable.
Implementation: Integrate a lightweight blockchain API (e.g., Hyperledger Fabric) to log transactions.
